My condolences to the families, friends and loved ones of those who've been killed by police

I freely gave more than 5 years of my life and more than 25,000 hours to this work.
I am unable to continue due to lack of support.

Many thanks to the very few who helped.

Please consider a parting gift as I attempt to find my way.

sol·i·dar·i·ty - kbp
